Heading: 2 MQTT Control Packet format -> 2.1 Structure of an MQTT Control Packet -> 2.1.2 MQTT Control Packet type
Sentence: Table 2-1 MQTT Control Packet types: Reserved (Value 0, Forbidden, Reserved), CONNECT (Value 1, Client to Server, Connection request), CONNACK (Value 2, Server to Client, Connect acknowledgment), PUBLISH (Value 3, Client to Server or Server to Client, Publish message), PUBACK (Value 4, Client to Server or Server to Client, Publish acknowledgment for QoS 1), PUBREC (Value 5, Client to Server or Server to Client, Publish received for QoS 2 delivery part 1), PUBREL (Value 6, Client to Server or Server to Client, Publish release for QoS 2 delivery part 2), PUBCOMP (Value 7, Client to Server or Server to Client, Publish complete for QoS 2 delivery part 3), SUBSCRIBE (Value 8, Client to Server, Subscribe request), SUBACK (Value 9, Server to Client, Subscribe acknowledgment), UNSUBSCRIBE (Value 10, Client to Server, Unsubscribe request), UNSUBACK (Value 11, Server to Client, Unsubscribe acknowledgment), PINGREQ (Value 12, Client to Server, PING request), PINGRESP (Value 13, Server to Client, PING response), DISCONNECT (Value 14, Client to Server or Server to Client, Disconnect notification), AUTH (Value 15, Client to Server or Server to Client, Authentication exchange).
